                lsp-exp 6 fc nc profile in
                lsp-exp 7 fc af profile in
            exit
            egress
                remarking
                fc af
                    dscp-in-profile cs5
                    dscp-out-profile cs5
                    lsp-exp-in-profile 5
                    lsp-exp-out-profile 5
                exit
                fc h1
                    dscp-in-profile cs4
                    dscp-out-profile cs4
                    lsp-exp-in-profile 4
                    lsp-exp-out-profile 4
                exit
                fc nc
                    dscp-in-profile nc1
                    dscp-out-profile nc1
                    lsp-exp-in-profile 6
                    lsp-exp-out-profile 6
                exit
            exit
        exit
    exit

                exit

                exit
                neighbor 218.74.122.2
                    description "to: LS-LS-CD-CR-1.MAN.CRS"
                exit
            exit
            no shutdown
        exit
    exit

echo "System Time NTP Configuration"

        time
